DeferredReason is a string that describes why a resource was deferred.\n   480→// It differs from the protobuf enum in that it adds more cases\n   481→// since it's more widely used to represent the reason for deferral.\n   482→// Reasons like instance count unknown and deferred prereq are not\n   483→// relevant for providers but can occur in general.\n   484→type DeferredReason string\n   485→\n   486→const (\n   487→\t// DeferredReasonInvalid is used when the reason for deferring is\n   488→\t// unknown or irrelevant.\n   489→\tDeferredReasonInvalid DeferredReason = \"invalid\"\n   490→\n   491→\t// DeferredReasonInstanceCountUnknown is used when the reason for deferring\n   492→\t// is that the count or for_each meta-attribute was unknown.\n   493→\tDeferredReasonInstanceCountUnknown DeferredReason = \"instance_count_unknown\"\n   494→\n   495→\t// DeferredReasonResourceConfigUnknown is used when the reason for deferring\n   496→\t// is that the resource configuration was unknown.\n   497→\tDeferredReasonResourceConfigUnknown DeferredReason = \"resource_config_unknown\"\n   498→\n   499→\t// DeferredReasonProviderConfigUnknown is 503→\t// DeferredReasonAbsentPrereq is used when the reason for deferring is that\n   504→\t// a required prerequisite resource was absent.\n   505→\tDeferredReasonAbsentPrereq DeferredReason = \"absent_prereq\"\n   506→\n   507→\t// DeferredReasonDeferredPrereq is used when the reason for deferring is\n   508→\t// that a required prerequisite resource was itself deferred.\n   509→\tDeferredReasonDeferredPrereq DeferredReason = \"deferred_prereq\"\n   510→)\n   511→\n   512→type Deferred struct {\n   513→\tReason DeferredReason\n   514→}\n   515→\n   516→type
